126→\tif len(requirements) == 0 {\n   127→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   128→\t}\n   129→\n   130→\treqs := make([]fields.Requirement, 0, len(requirements))\n   131→\tvar errs []error\n   132→\tfor _, expr expr.Values[0]})\n   153→\t\tcase metav1.FieldSelectorOpExists, metav1.FieldSelectorOpDoesNotExist:\n   154→\t\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"fieldSelectors do not yet support %v\", together to enforce role-based access control:\\n\\n## Core Authorization Logic\\n\\n**RBACAuthorizer** (`plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/rbac.go`): The main authorizer implementing the `authorizer.Authorizer` interface. **SubjectAccessReview** (`pkg/registry/authorization/subjectaccessreview/rest.go`): Cluster-scoped access review\\n- **LocalSubjectAccessReview** (`pkg/registry/authorization/localsubjectaccessreview/rest.go`): Namespace-scoped access review\\n- **SelfSubjectAccessReview** (`pkg/registry/authorization/selfsubjectaccessreview/rest.go`): Check (`pkg/registry/authorization/rest/storage_authorization.go`): Registers these handlers\\n\\n## Bootstrap RBAC Policies\\n\\nInitial RBAC policy definitions are provided by:\\n- `policy.go`: Defines system ClusterRoles and ClusterRoleBindings (including system:admin, system:nodes, etc.)\\n- `namespace_policy.go`: Provides namespace-scoped Roles and RoleBindings (e.g., edit, view roles)\\n- `controller_policy.go`: Defines roles for system controllers\\n\\nThese are reconciled during API server startup via the PostStartHook mechanism in `pkg/registry/rbac/rest/storage_rbac.go`.\\n\\n## (`pkg/registry/rbac/role/policybased/storage.go`): Wraps standard storage to validate that users cannot grant themselves permissions they don't already have\\n- **ClusterRole** (`pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrole/policybased/storage.go`): Validates escalation, including aggregation rules\\n- **RoleBinding** (`pkg/registry/rbac/rolebinding/policybased/storage.go`): Checks binding authorization\\n- **ClusterRoleBinding** (`pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrolebinding/policybased/storage.go`): Checks binding authorization at cluster scope\\n\\nAll storage implementations use:\\n- rules\\n\\nThese mechanisms ensure that users can only create or modify roles/bindings if they already possess all permissions being granted.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
